 vittamantri ne pitiai ke saath baatcheet main kaha, maafee yojana kaa koi maamla hi nahin banataa, kyonki ek laghu varg ko chhodkar jo karmukt he, ab lagbhag sabhi ritern online daakhil kiye ja rahe hai

 unhone kaha, main logon se kahana chaahunga ki kripaya apni aay na chhipaaen

 chidambaram ne kaha ki bajet main ek khaas tabake ko chhodkar kisi bhi varg ke logon par koi atirikt kar bhaar nahin daalaa gaya
 Only a small burden of 10 percent surcharge has been imposed on the affluent 42,800 people in the income bracket of more than Rs 1 crore annually
 vittamantri ne is ashanka ko khaarij kiya ki dhani vyaktiyon par lagaaya gaya yah adhibhaar kar ek saal se adhik jari rah saktaa he
 Chidambaram said, surcharges have been imposed in the past and have been abolished
 unhone banking nakadi lenden kar or seemaant laabhkar hataae jane kaa udhaaharan diya, jinhen kuch saal pehle ke bajaton main khatm kar diya gaya

 unhone kaha, koi bhi kahin nahin jayega

 jin logon ko notice bheje gaye hai, unhen unke kharch or kharid ke bare main bataaya gaya he

" isliye, agar iskar ritern se praapt soochna anya sroton se mili soochna se mail nahin khaati he, to us par kaam kiya jayega

 Chidambaram said, the income of the top 10 percent of the population can be quite high

 bahupratikshit 'humsafar express' train shuukravaar ko nai dilli se shuru kii jaaegi
 Flexi fare will be applicable for this train with many facilities
 flixi fere system yani kam hoti siton ke saath badhata kiraaya
 It will have all coaches AC-3
 chunki yah train coffee, chaay, soup vending mashin se yukt he or prayek cabin main refriorated pentry tathaa anya suvidhaayen maujuud hai, isliye yatriyon ko saamaanya mail, express asi-3 ke mukaable aadhaar kiraye ke taur par 1
 15% higher rent will have to be paid
 ek senior railway afasar ke mutabik, normal AC kochon kii tulana main modern facelity vaale in kochon kii nirmaan laagat zyada he
 In this case, special fairs are kept
 railmantri suresh prabhu video conferencing ke jariye gorakhpur-anand vihaar ke bich purna asi-3 seva kaa udghaatan karenge
 It is worth noting that in the Railway Budget last year, Railway Minister Suresh Prabhu announced Humsafar Train
 isamen sabhi coach asi-3 category ke honge
 It will have CCTV, gps-based passenger information system, fire and smoke detection and suppression system
 humsafar ke coach maharaja express ke coach kii tarah honge
 Since this train is equipped with coffee, tea, soup vending machines and each cabin has a refrigerated pantry and other facilities, the passengers are charged 1 as base fare as against the normal mail, express AC-3
 15 fisadi adhik kiraaya dena hoga
 According to a senior railway officer, the cost of manufacturing of these coaches with modern facility is higher as compared to the normal AC coaches
 aise main special fares rakhe gaye hai
 Railway Minister Suresh Prabhu will inaugurate the full AC-3 service between gorakhpur-anand Vihar through video conferencing
 gauratlab he ki beete saal rail bajet main rail mantri suresh prabhu ne humsafar train kaa elaan kiya tha
 All coaches will be in the AC-3 category
 isamen sisitivi, jeepies-besd paisangers information system, fire or smoke ditection or sapressant system rahegaa
 Humsafar coaches will be like the coaches of Maharaja Express

 gadakari ne is baat kii pairvi kii he ki centre main laal batti kii suvidha raashtrapati, uparashtrapati, pradhanmantri, supreme court ke mukhya nyaayadhish or loksabhaa ke spikar ko hi di jaae, jabaki rajyon main yah suvidha mukhyamantri, rajyapal, hycourt ke mukhya nyaayadhish ke saath keval vidhansabha ke spikar ko di jaae

 bihar main richter scale par 5
 The tremors of a magnitude 7 earthquake rocked people on Saturday evening
 bihar ke alaava is bukamp ke jatke padosi rajya pashchim bengal or sikkim main bhi mahasoos kiye gaye
 Due to the earthquake, one person died after the wall of a house collapsed in Shikarpur in West Champaran district
 pashchim champaran jile ke ek adhikari ne bataaya ki is bukamp kii vajah se jile ke shikarpur kshetra main ek ghar gir jane se ek vyakti kii maut hui he
 At the same time, Director of the Indian Meteorological Department AK Sen told that 5 pm
 04 baje rajdhani patna sahit pradesh ke mujffarpur, madhubani, kishanganj, purvi champaran, lakhisarai, munger jilon sahit rajya ke anya bhaagon main richter paimaane par 5
 7 earthquake tremors were felt
 unhone bataaya ki is bukamp kaa centre padosi desh nepal main tha
 Sen reported that 9 this morning

 vittamantri pi chidambaram ne sanket diya ki arthvyavastha ke samaksh chunautiyon ke chalate unke haath band hue the, haalanki sansad main bajet paarit hone ke dauraan or kadamon tathaa faislon kii ghoshnaa kii jaaegi
 In the formal press conference after presenting the general budget, he said that the budget is not a one-time thing or a single step, it is a continuous process
 unhone kaha, vastav main arthvyavastha ke samaksh chunautiyaan hai or ye chunautiyaan kai tarah kii hai
 These challenges are mentioned in the Economic Review
 sansad main bajet charchaa tathaa vitt vidheyak par jawaab main or faislon va kadamon kii ghoshnaa kii jaaegi
 Justifying the 10 per cent surcharge on rich or super-rich people, Chidambaram said that this step has been taken for one year only because there is pressure on revenue and we have to reduce the fiscal deficit to 4 in 2013-14
 8 pratishat par laana he
 He said, once the tax revenue increases, after one year we will not need surcharge
 yah to pul kii tarah he
 Chidambaram objected to the media linking the definition of super-rich to those with income above Rs 1 crore and said, "I did not use the word super-rich"
 unhone kaha ki adhibhaar se kar chori ko badhaava nahin milegaa
 The finance minister said that the budget estimated a gain of Rs 13,300 crore from direct taxes will come from a 10 per cent surcharge on the wealthy income tax payers (with annual income of Rs 1 crore or more)
 desh main is varg ke logon kii sankhya 42,800 he
 He said that the budget has not put any burden on the people nor has it scared the market and any section of investors
 chidambaram ne kaha, bajet kaa mukhya jor rajkoshiya samajhadaari vaala maarg apnaanaa tathaa rajkoshiya ghate ko is saal 5
 2 percent and 4 next year
 8 pratishat par niyantrit rakhana he
 Asked about the criticism of the budget by the UPA constituents such as the SP, Chidambaram said he was confident that the Budget and Finance Bill would be passed in Parliament
 vittamantri ne kaha ki vah bajet ko janvirohi tathaa kisaan virdohi bataane sambandhi sari aalochanaon kaa jawaab sansad main denge
 He said, earlier the budget of the government has been passed
 tippaniyan Chidambaram said that the government is aiming to get Rs 40,000 crore from disinvestment in the coming financial year and Rs 14,000 crore from the sale of the government's remaining stake in non-government companies like Balco and HZL
 unhone maujuuda chaalu khaataa ghate ko jatil mudda bataaya, kyonki aayaat, niryaat kii tulana main kaaphi adhik he
 He said that the only way to overcome CAD at medium and long term level is to increase exports, as the import of oil and food cannot be eliminated
 chidambaram ne ummid jataai ki vruddhi, mudrasphiti niyantran tathaa nivesh ke lihaaj se aagaamee vittvarsh maujuuda 2012-13 kii tulana main behatar hoga
 He said that 6 in 2013–14

 After achieving a growth rate of 7 percent, the economic growth rate in 2014-15 should be more than seven percent
 aam bajet pesh karne ke baad aupchaarik samvaadadaata sammelan main unhone kaha ki bajet koi ekbargi kii baat yaa akelaa kadam nahin he, yah to satat prakriya he
 He said, there are indeed challenges before the economy and these challenges are many
 aarthik samiksha main in chunautiyon kaa zikr he

 8 percent
 unhone kaha, ek baar kar rajasav badhane par ek saal baad hamen adhibhaar kii jarurat nahin hogi
 It is like a bridge
 chidambaram ne media dwaara super-rich kii paribhaasha ko keval ek karod rupee se adhik aay waalon se jodne par aapatti jataai or kaha, maine super-rich shabd kaa istemaal nahin kiya
 He said the surcharge would not lead to tax evasion
 vittamantri ne kaha ki bajet main pratyaksh karon se 13,300 karod rupee ke laabh kaa jo anumaan lagaaya gaya he, uskaa bada hissaa dhanadhy iskar daataaon (ek karod rupee yaa usase adhik kii salanaa aay waalon) par 10 pratishat adhibhaar se aayega
 There are 42,800 people in this class in the country
 unhone kaha ki bajet ne logon par koi boj nahin daalaa he or na hi bazaar tathaa niveshkon ke kisi varg ko daraaya he
 Chidambaram said, the main thrust of the budget is to adopt fiscal prudent path and fiscal deficit this year
5
 2 pratishat tathaa agle saal 4
 8 percent to be controlled

 The Finance Minister said that he will answer all the criticisms regarding the budget as anti-people and anti-farmer
 unhone kaha, pehle bhi sarkaar ke bajet paarit hue hai
 The comments chidambaram ne kaha ki sarkaar aagaamee vittvarsh main vinievesh se 40,000 karod rupee tathaa balko or echjedel jaisi gaiyr-sarkari companiyon main sarkaar kii baaki hissedari briki se 14,000 karod rupee hasil karne kaa lakshya lekar chal rahi he
 He described the current current account deficit as a complex issue, as imports are much higher than exports
